The nose behind this fragrance is Daniela Andrier. Top notes are Neroli, Black Pepper, Cardamom and Carrot Seeds; middle notes are Iris, Violet, Geranium and Mate; base notes are Amber, Cedar, Sandalwood and Patchouli. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>The house of Prada launches La Femme Prada and L'Homme Prada mid-2016. The new fragrant “pair of equals" represents man and woman that are “reunited in an identical vision. She could be him, he could be her. She is an absolute woman, he is an absolute man. There is not an obvious definition of relationship between them. They could be lovers, friends, or even strangers. Both have multiple identities.“ </p>

<p>L'Homme Prada is a modern scent that combines the classic Prada ingredients - amber and iris. There are also notes of neroli, geranium and patchouli. The character of the fragrance is described as airy, reserved and challenging. Available as a 50 and 100 ml Eau de Toilette.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2319661" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="FrogLog"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2203922"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2203922.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="FrogLog" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2319661ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2319661" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2203922">FrogLog</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-18">10/18/24 07:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Smells like the lather of white bar soap in your room at an expensive hotel while wearing a clean white t shirt fresh out of the dryer.<br />
 <br />
Super clean and soapy and smells extremely pleasant. <br />
<br />
The iris doesn't give it the lipsticky/makeup bag scent that something like Dior Homme Intense might. It's blended into a more powdery soapy fragrance, but it is still discernably iris forward. The woody accord is very light compared to the darker, thicker DHI, so it is a more light, airy, and powdery perfume. <br />
<br />
Not powdery like your grandma's foundation makeup, but like white bar soap. Soft, clean, an creamy powdery.<br />
<br />
Can't overspray<br />
Safe blind buy<br />
Duration and sillage better than expected<br />
Everyone loves it<br />
I want to bathe in it</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2319661"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2319661#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2319552" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2208865">axelcervantesml</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-18">10/18/24 04:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Powdery, floral, and very polite-smelling. However, there's sharpness to it, almost screechy floral note, probably the iris very much forwarded. That's whats gonna turn heads for you with this fragrance, but I can imagine very few people will turn their heads the bad way.<br />
<br />
Now for the price, at least where I live, it costs way too much and I'd rather go for something like Burberry Touch, half the price of this, if I'm looking to get the same vibe. I would consider this a masterpiece as many others do. So versatile yet full of character, never offensive and never overwhelming yet so distinct. I find it to be the perfect scent for ANYBODY.<br />
<br />
Calling this masculine is a cope however. Its extremely unisex and only the first minute could be considered masculine. Theres nothing wrong with men wearing non masculine perfume. I think guys especially have to realize that… i could see an extremely girly woman wearing this just as much as a hairy muscular bear<br />
<br />
Calling this perfume ‘floral’ is pushing it tho. Iris doesnt smell floral at all and violet smells more crisp sweet woody and textural to me. The end result is a light indigo colored powder bomb with tiny pale chartreuse dots scattered in the background<br />
<br />
Performance is perfect i think. It lasts but it doesnt project too much. <br />
<br />
The balance between violet and crispy green notes is really nice. It creates a freshness without being sharp and citrusy. More like fresh spring air. Definitely recommending to anyone</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2311830"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2311830#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2310379" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; But I still will grab for it in certain instances.   For instance,  took a shower at like 4 pm…. Wanted something clean and fresh without screaming citrus or barbershop notes.  I wanted it to be crowd friendly while I was in rehearsal…. And not too loud.  Something on the softer and clean side.<br />
<br />
It’s powdery for sure…. Almost so much that there is a “tipping point” for me.   3-4 sprays is enough.  Go for that 5th spray and it’s instantly a headache inducer.<br />
<br />
The fragrance is well done, I like it on occasion, but it’s definitely not a daily wear.  <br />
<br />
The fragrance LONGEVITY lasts and lasts and lasts!   It never disappears. <br />
<br />
Day or night….. most any season (yet, I would NEVER wear this in the southern heat and humidity during the summer). <br />
<br />
Would I purchase it again?   Probably not.   But I have a huge bottle…. So it will be around for a while.<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2287056" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="xkcls350"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1270148"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="xkcls350" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2287056ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2287056" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1270148">xkcls350</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-18">09/18/24 10:25</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Prada L'Homme is a standout fragrance for anyone seeking a fresh and clean scent. From the moment you apply it, you're enveloped in a soapy aroma that feels like your clothes have just come out of the washing machine—clean, crisp, and refreshing. This makes it an ideal choice for daily wear, especially as an office scent, or even for casual evenings.<br />
<br />
The longevity is above average, offering a solid 6-10 hours on the skin, which is impressive for an Eau de Toilette. The sillage, while not the strongest, is still quite respectable, projecting enough to leave a pleasant trail without overwhelming those around you.<br />
<br />
Prada L'Homme is particularly well-suited for younger individuals, as its fresh, versatile profile makes it a safe, crowd-pleasing option for almost any occasion. If you're looking for a reliable fragrance that delivers on cleanliness and sophistication, this one is definitely worth considering.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; The pepper is pretty potent in the first few minutes of spraying, but dries down releaitvely quickly to that powdery, soapy scent that is reminiscent of clean laundry. Can see this working in any everyday setting, as others have said this is an extravagant office fragrance.<br />
<br />
Projection is nice, I've personally gone noseblind because of how much I've used it this summer but you'll get good compliments from people around you. Longevity is also pretty nice, on my skin I get around 6hrs of projection, with it becoming a skin scent for the next hour or two. I'd say it leans more toward spring/summer, but it's clean and safe enough to rock in the fall, and even in the warmer winter days.<br />
<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2263039" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="coolgene"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2234758"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2234758.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="coolgene" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Etat-Libre-d-Orange/Experimentum-Crucis-54453.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.54453.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Experimentum Crucis"title="Experimentum Crucis"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2263039ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2263039" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2234758">coolgene</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-27">08/27/24 17:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Prada L’Homme is one of my go-to scents for the office. It’s effortlessly clean and sophisticated, perfect for professional settings where you want to smell good without drawing too much attention.<br />
<br />
This fragrance has a distinct, soapy vibe, which I find pleasant. It’s got that just-out-of-the-shower freshness that’s hard to beat. While it’s great for daytime wear, especially at work, I wouldn’t reach for it on a date night. It’s more about projecting a polished, professional image than creating a mood.<br />
<br />
In terms of performance, Prada L’Homme is pretty balanced. The projection is moderate, so it’s noticeable without overpowering, which is what you want in a workplace setting. Longevity is solid, lasting through a typical workday, and the sillage is just right—enough to leave a clean, subtle trail without being intrusive.<br />
<br />
Overall, if you’re looking for a safe, refined, and perfectly suited fragrance for the office, Prada L’Homme is a great choice. Its scent keeps you smelling fresh and put together all day.<br />
<br />
Key Points:<br />
<br />
	•	Office Wear: Ideal for professional settings; clean and sophisticated.<br />
	•	Scent Profile: Soapy and fresh with a pleasant, polished vibe.<br />
	•	Performance: Moderate projection, good longevity, and subtle sillage—perfect for a work environment.<br />
	•	Occasion: Best for daytime wear, especially in professional settings; not something I’d pick for a night out.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2263039"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2263039#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2262819" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; frag works best when worn during the day. the dry down transitions to the creamy notes. feels and smells like good lotion.<br />
<br />
not offensive and very pleasant to wear when you are in a situation where there is always someone beside you.<br />
<br />
library/school/office friendly.<br />
<br />
10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2244515"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2244515#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2243919" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Luckily the muskiness slightly outweighs the floral so that it still leans masculine, but it could come off as unisex to some. There's a little soapiness but laundry detergent? Only if it's like some very rich super niche detergent with flecks of silver that only billionaires can afford. Someone else said Lysol crisp linen scent and I tested them side by side for the heck of it and it's not even close.<br />
Overall, not an every day scent for me (my attire is business casual), but a very elegant, pleasant, and classy scent for more formal occasions, BOTH day and night. Doesn't seem to project too too much on my skin, but I understand it's not meant to be a room filler. Helps confidently check off the box for the more formal and/or iris corner of the collection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2243919"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2243919#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2243909" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2108424">Cosmos_PMF</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-20">07/20/24 05:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is the best office/elegant daytime fragrance ever created. Absolute masterpiece.<br />
<br />
I used to test this in stores several times and I remember the first time I tried it on I didn't like it, I didn't own any powdery fragrance back then.<br />
Again again and again more wears from stores like Sephora and I ended up liking it a lot, has grown on me perfectly.<br />
I went on a trip in Barcelona recently and picked it up with a discounted price (50ml). Blown away.<br />
<br />
The scent profile is soapy, powdery, as how Jeremy says "luxurious hotel soap". It smells a bit like a makeup kit or lipstick, but in the sexiest most professional way possible<br />
If you prefer iris scents and you wanna feel and smell as clean as possible, then you're gonna love this stuff a lot. It's not a love at first sniff, take your time and you can even sample it, not really begginer friendly scent since there are gonna be people finding this smelling too feminine.<br />
Iris, neroli, amber. Smooth as hell. <br />
<br />
The performance is this is so weird to explain. I have the new Made in France batch which people complain it lasts a very little time on their skin and the reformulation ruined the cologne.<br />
But man, I literally get 8-10hrs of this with a medium projection, not sure what to say since the batch is for sure the reformulated version of it. Maybe it's my skin carrying powdery scents more than others.<br />
<br />
About versatility, I feel like if you use Prada L Homme while wearing a dress shirt or a polo in any environment apart from clubbing, girls cannot stand you. You smell like a gentleman with manners in a professional way, more mature if you pull it off.<br />
Spring-Summer-Fall/Autumn, daytime scent. <br />
<br />
The bottle is perfect. It's designed exactly how every fragrance is held by a human's hand, offering an amazing grip experience. Very nice back material. <br />
<br />
I do love Prada L Homme Intense too, its a more rugged leather-ish version of Prada L Homme and it's an evening time scent. I feel your collection would already be complete if you own the original and the intense version, one for daytime one for night outs. I'm for real.<br />
<br />
In my top 5 all time fav designer fragrances.<br />
<br />
Prada L'Homme: powdery, soapy, elegant, versatile, professional. Wear it with confidence. A masterpiece. 9.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2224151"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2224151#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2222983" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1701040">stardust_ziggy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-04">07/04/24 07:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Be clean, groomed, well dressed. Spray this on and go shopping for yachts. They could charge so much more for this wonderful 10/10 scent, I truly love it. <br />
<br />
When you first spray it, you get this fresh and slightly spicy kick from the neroli and black pepper, with a hint of cardamom and carrot seeds adding some depth. It’s like a crisp, clean start that feels really modern.<br />
<br />
As it settles, you start to notice the heart of the fragrance, where iris really shines. The iris gives it this powdery, almost creamy quality that feels incredibly luxurious. There are also touches of violet and geranium that add a subtle floral sweetness, balanced perfectly by a green, slightly herbal note from the mate.<br />
<br />
Finally, it dries down into this warm, inviting base of amber, cedar, patchouli, and sandalwood. It’s smooth and comforting, with just enough depth to keep it interesting without being overpowering. The whole experience feels very refined and polished, like wearing a perfectly tailored suit. It’s definitely a scent that makes a statement of quiet confidence and sophistication.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2207966"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2207966#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2207161" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I asked my two year old son his thoughts on this and he said “This is a true artistic masterpiece, a perfectly balanced composition of powdery, creamy iris intertwined amongst elegant, white florals. Exquisite”</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2186357"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2186357#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2185976" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2183441" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="WesFragrance"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2139143"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2139143.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="WesFragrance" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2183441ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2183441" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2139143">WesFragrance</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-09">06/09/24 20:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My wife bought me this bottle upon release in 2016 and I immediately loved it. After recently getting back into fragrances it's one that kept coming back to mind. I sampled it again the other night while shopping, it's as beautiful and elegant as I remembered.<br />
<br />
For me, this is a nice change from a lot of the mainstream designer fragrances that feature a fresh citrus blast, followed by woody, spicy undertones. Prada L'homme smells like freshly picked iris with a soapy, powdery, freshly washed clothes lingering in the background. It's unique in it's own way and won't appeal to everyone but for those that like this scent profile I feel it's a must for any collection. <br />
<br />
I also compared this sample directly with Amourage Reflection, while Reflection Man has more depth and character, Prada plays in it's own simplified space and held it's own against the much more expensive fragrance. I love both these fragrances, if I had to own one it would be Prada L'homme once price was factored in, take price out of the equation then it's Reflection Man by a small margin.  <br />
<br />
This is a great office, daily scent and wouldn't be out of place for date nights and cuddles with your partner on the couch. Extremely versatile. <br />
<br />
Sillage and projection is pretty much spot on, it's loud enough to get noticed but won't stink out an entire room and start giving people headaches. <br />
<br />
Performance, while it did fade off my skin after around 6-7 hours I could still smell it on my jumper the next day, no issues there, solid performer. <br />
<br />
This is absolutely on my want list and will be buying a bottle soon.<br />
<br />
Overall 9.1/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2183441"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2183441#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2183364" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It is disappointing because I miss Prada putting out good soap fragrances such as Prada Amber Pour Homme, or even this one. But now they just focus on “Luna Rossa Ocean” which I don’t get the appeal.<br />
<br />
Prada L’Homme is nevertheless, a great fragrance, my signature scent back in Pre-Med. I got many compliments from my fellow students and some patients during my internship days. I love this fragrance as it hold a sentimental value of my Pre-Med. It is professional and clean smelling, it is comfortable, unique and soft, which is appropriate for the work environment especially when I’m handling patients, they never found it repulsive nor headache inducing, more or less it is just soft and comfy fragrance. Overall still a great fragrance for me, but sadly it doesn’t last as long as it used to, and I fear this might get discontinued, hopefully not. <br />
<br />
I still hold it in a pedestal, but ever since they changed houses to L’Oreal, the releases of Prada Fragrances, majority what L’Oreal releases are just utter boring and mainstream, I mean look what they had done to YSL Y elixir, piece of hot expensive garbage if you ask me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It's absolutely one of my new favorites and stood out among a set of both designer and niche decants. Like many other EDTs, this fragrance explodes off of me for about the first hour, but it is so non offensive, even my more discerning coworkers didn't mind and/or enjoyed the sillage. Like many other EDTs, this only projects for about 3-4 hours on my skin, but then unless you stuff your face into it, it's undetectable.<br />
Still, this blend is so enjoyable and so versatile I've ordered a full bottle before even finishing my sample. And about it not being "masculine" enough, I've smelled plenty of niche frags that "leaned masculine" that are much more feminine than this. Edit: i bought Dior Homme Intense and sold this to my dad as he really liked it and i think it suits him more</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2153603"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2153603#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2152042" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Upon spraying it, I noticed how it has a bit of a barbershop/oldschool vibe with iris and powdery floral notes and in the drydown it turns into heaven. Clean, sophisticated, soapy, soft, but still carries that masculine edge on a very elevated level. This has to be the best Prada fragrance besides its Intense flanker. I cannot say enough good things about this scent profile.<br />
Unfortunately though, weak formulation got to this beauty too, so performance is not the best, especially with newer batches. But this doesn't need to be loud at all.<br />
I have to give it a 9/10 excluding performance, because I just love this scent so much.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2152042"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2152042#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2150847" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It is now made in France for the past few years. I have multiple bottles of both versions and it’s a night and day difference, although they smell identical. Two sprays with the made in Spain version is all you need for all day long. With the made in France you need to reapply every few hours.<br />
<br />
This is the fragrance that got me into fragrances, but it’s such a shame that the longevity is no longer there though. If you are lucky enough to snag a bottle of the made in Spain version, it’s well worth it even if it’s double/triple the price. <br />
<br />
10/10 - made in Spain<br />
7/10 - made in France</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2148975"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2148975#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2147846" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; A light scent that doesn’t hit people in the face when you walk by. I would say it doesn’t project much but what it does best in is leave a trail. Also awesome in semi-formal to formal events. It’s not a fresh scent but rather a light and clean scent making it unique compared to other fragrance houses. When I smell this it reminds me of sniffing flowers with a light breeze in a back yard with clean bedsheets no hanging to dry. This leans masculine. With some of the best ingredients I’ve seen for a designer cologne. 4 for office but if you have fragrance strict work policies 3 sprays will do. <br />
Scent: 9/10 <br />
Longevity 10/10 best EDT longevity I’ve smelled <br />
Projection 7/10  <br />
Unique: 8.5/10 niche worthy <br />
Price: 8/10 <br />
Overall:9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2141607"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2141607#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2141569" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Here's why:<br />
<br />
1. Not everything needs to be a projection beast. Most people don't want to smell you that much anyway.<br />
<br />
2. People forget that simply smelling clean and respectable is extremely sexy to most people - this is the epitome of clean, respectful and sophisticated.<br />
<br />
3. Sometimes it's nice to have a fragrance that doesn't obviously smell like a fragrance. Rather than being an obvious fragrance, you will instead, create an aura of elegance. You'll just smell sophisticated and put together.<br />
<br />
Prada L'Homme is excellent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2136515"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2136515#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2135330" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1726328">Unclespacey</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-24">04/24/24 09:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I have to admit I’m not a big fan of the opening. It reminds me of Gentleman edp and NR bleu noir Parfum, both of which were repulsive to my nose, way too mature, and I gave both of them away. But after about 30 minutes, that iris note gets pushed to the background and it becomes a clean, soapy, somewhat sweet floral fragrance that is absolutely beautiful. I actually didn’t know what I was smelling for a little while, until I figured out it was myself. I see now why this is called the office king. Perfect for a business casual setting, year round. I’m sure the iris note would be cloying in the high heat, but if you’re in a climate controlled environment, this is the perfect fragrance for every day. As a 30yo male, I wouldn’t recommend this to the younger fellows. Iris fragrances in general are too mature for my taste, but the dry down of this fragrance is just so lovely.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2134927"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2134927#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2134315" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

I don't get the laundry sheet vibe some mention - I think it's a bit too luxurious for that, but there is a slight "sophisticated" soapiness which wears well all day. Longevity is good (six hours or so), sillage is solid and the price is certainly right. I'll definitely try the Intense version as I'm curious about a "darker" interpretation, but until then this is a go-to fragrance when you've got to be "forward facing" for the day.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2126072"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2126072#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2123837" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2123837" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ivanthegreat"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2094715"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="ivanthegreat" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2123837ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2123837" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2094715">ivanthegreat</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-13">04/13/24 13:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I’ve heard people describe this scent as a powdery, luxury laundry detergent and I agree. It smells so clean and wonderful. Even if I couldn’t wear this I would still buy it just to be able to smell that beautiful scent from the atomizer. I’ve previously stated how much I detest the note of iris in fragrances but it’s totally different in this. It’s toned down so much and blended so well with the other ingredients. It’s not the powerful and nauseating type of iris that’s present in other men’s fragrances. It’s true that performance isn’t beast mode but on my skin it’s actually not weak. I get about 5 hours of projection and it stays on me as a skin scent for another 4 hours.<br />
This stuff is such a legendary office/classroom fragrance. There is a 0% chance you will choke out or offend anyone with this. <br />
Another thing I’ve heard guys say is why would they want to smell like clean soap if they’re trying to attract women. I don’t think guys realize that there are many women out there that really really appreciate a clean smelling guy. Not every woman wants you to smell like an apple pie or a sweet vanilla fragrance. As for the Intense version, the benefit is that it has way better performance but the downsides (for me at least) are that the iris note is turned way up, it’s more expensive, and the stronger performance makes it a worse office/classroom fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I got a bottle of this second-hand after hearing that it’s a very clean, soapy, borderline unisex scent. I do have to say it’s probably my most masculine-leaning “unisex” cologne due to some of the notes, but also strangely soft and powdery? I feel like it’s how I would smell if I showered with a hyper-feminine floral shampoo, used my husband’s fresh/spicy body wash, and then layered on a soft, powdery body cream.  <br />
It totally does dry down to a fabric softener type scent, creamy and powdery with a touch of florals/spice. I feel like a soft feminine girly would probably not love this - I picture more of a femme fatale rocking this (probably due to the masculine leaning notes), like a striking brunette with high cheekbones and a slicked back bun, wearing a leather jacket and high heeled boots kinda vibe, strutting around in boss mode. <br />
Definitely soapy/laundry clean but has some bite. <br />
<br />
For reference, other “unisex” (or just not super feminine) scents I like are Commodity Book, Commodity Moss, Jo Malone Wood Sage Sea Salt, MMM By the Fireplace &amp; Jazz Club, Penhaglions Castile, Maison Louie Marie Bois de Balincourt, Clean Reserve Citron Fig… <br />
<br />
Also - I’ve been hearing Amber L’Homme is more soapy, can anyone confirm this? I’m always on the hunt for a “bar of soap in a bottle”.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2114527"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2114527#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2113838" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1654692">MiiiL33</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-02">04/02/24 11:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Edit 06/29/2024:<br />
I've been using it more and more, I absolutely love this! The maceration is very important as from the first use, the projection and sillage were terrible, they went only up as time passed. One of the best of my collection 💛<br />
----<br />
First of all, I think that the scent is great. It is clean, sweet but not cloying, an everyday scent. I can make comparisions to Dior Homme Eau for Men in the fresh side: they are somewhat similar, with the same profile as an iris freshie. Dior has the citrus side and Prada has the powdery side. Also, similarities with L'homme Intense are notorious, as the iris note is dominant in both fragrances, just that L'homme has the freshness of neroli and Intense is more leathery.<br />
I've been very hyped about this fragrance, but when I got it I was very dissapointed with its projection and longevity. Yesterday when I first sprayed on me, it lasted no more than an hour and the sillage was ridiculously low, I even oversprayed with more than 15 times and reapplied around 3 or 4 times. Today, I've applied on me and the longevity has been better, I sprayed at 8 am and now at 3 pm and I can get some whiffs close to my arm. This is a very beautiful fragrance, I just think that the curse of newer batches is real: they tend to last shorter, performance is not as good as the original. My advice to you is that if you want this fragrance, try getting an older batch, or look the package that says Made in Spain. The Made in France batches of Prada tends to be a lot worse than Spain batches.<br />
Scent: 9/10<br />
Projection: 5/10<br />
Batch 22X71C6, by L'Oreal. Production date: 2023-09</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2111968"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2111968#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2110422" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I believe that label diminishes the true essence and character of this fragrance.  I'm quite sure the house of Prada sought higher accolades with the launch of this gem.  Prada L'Homme is posh, elegant, refined, high quality, and very well blended.  This scent exudes class and shines far beyond the office/work setting.  It's profile, performance and versatility make it an any season, year-round fragrance.  At the price point that it can be acquired, you can't go wrong with adding this to your fragrance wardrobe.  I highly recommend giving it a try while it is still available.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2104320"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2104320#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2102676" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2102676" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Mattyp1124"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2065980"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Mattyp1124" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2102676ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2102676" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2065980">Mattyp1124</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-24">03/24/24 10:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Persoanlly, I think this is a very safe fragrance to wear. I have worn it alot recently to events and its great due to its inoffensive nature and how easy it is to wear. I can see where some people come saying its a bit feminine, but I think it really depends on how you put your style together when wearing this fragrance. For example, this fragrance does great in a suit and tie and feels very "put together" and more masculine when doing so. However, wearing this fragrance with shorts on while at a beach may be seen as more feminine and it makes sense. I think the best place for this fragrance would be the office as it is very light and is not going to cause issues for anyone. It smells like a fresh and slightly powdery high end soap, or even fabric softener. It opens with a very soft and slightly sweet spice (very light spice) but instantly dries into more of a smooth powdery scent. After a while, it dries down even more to the base notes which are very light and smooth, reminding me of a synthetic marshmellow scent (in the best way possible). Overall I give this fragrance an 8/10 due ot its versatility and inoffesnive nature, I surprisingly get over 8 hours of this on my skin (which becomes very faint after 8 hours) and I find it projects well, above average compared to other fragrances. <br />
If your looking for something soft and a bit sweet that would be mass appealing in most occasions, this is a great option for your.<br />
Thanks for reading, hope your having a great day.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2102676"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2102676#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2102208" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1742070">Shinic0d3</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-19">03/19/24 06:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Had this one for quite some time. Initial reactions to it when I tried it in the store was interesting, inoffensive, elegant, perfect office scent imho that's clean but very nice floral smelling, soapy and powdery. It's an Iris bomb though, if you overspray it it can become a bit too much, so I usually put on 3-4 sprays and keep it at that. 2 maybe if going to office and I know I'd be in meeting rooms whole day, not to annoy people around me. <br />
<br />
In terms of silage, not really the strongest, lasts around 6 hours on my skin, on clothes I can def smell it way longer. But I think that Iris is to my nose quite a strong scent, and I go nose blind from it fairly fast. I think that it's actually lasting a bit longer than what I experience (at least my wife can smell it on me when I can't). I'd wear this even at home office. In regards of seasons when to wear this, def Spring / Summer &amp; maybe Fall scent. Personally for fall I'd go with other spicier fragrances, but in general you can go with this whole year. It's really great scent if you want to smell nice, inoffensive, elegant. Totally recommend!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2097143"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2097143#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2095195" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1796349">Towels</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-10">03/10/24 23:10</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Most of the things you've read about this fragrance are correct. Floral, soapy, inoffensive, easy to wear. It really is lovely. Very beautiful fragrance. This is one of those fragrances where if you spray lightly, you can almost get away with not even giving the impression you've sprayed yourself with anything. It will just be a floral, soapy aura around you or if someone gets close. And I think that's really where this fragrance shines. It just kind of floats around you here and there. Very nice. <br />
<br />
Performance/projection: I can do just one spray and I smell it for many hours and even after I sleep when I wake up in the morning, can still get wafts of this. I've sprayed it on my shirt and it literally lasts for days. Again this is just one or two sprays. <br />
<br />
People could call this generic, boring, etc. But the truth is this is a masterpiece. It's just so pleasant and very, very high quality. Soapy and luxurious. And one of the few floral scents that actually smells very nice for a man. Please understand this is not supposed to fill a room or choke people out. This is not beast mode or to go clubbing or anything like that. This is just supposed to create a pleasant little bubble in your space. And if used correctly, it will draw people in.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="2088667"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=2088667#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2087183" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1416172">NoseBlindNJ</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-04-27">04/27/22 12:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is the first review I’ve done where I clicked on the smiley face with heart eyes. <br />
<br />
Prada L’Homme is in the top 3 fragrances I’ve EVER smelled. <br />
<br />
Some guys say this isn’t what a “man” should smell like- They must be drinking toilet water.  <br />
<br />
This is what you wear when you are going to meet the parents of the woman you are thinking of marrying. <br />
This smells clean and classy.  Not like “I’m here to chew gum and bang your daughter, and I’m all out of gum” <br />
<br />
You don’t picture a man with piercings in his face and tons of tattoos wearing this.  This fragrance says the opposite of “I’m a wild man” <br />
<br />
This is what you want your oncologist to smell like, or your pilot. <br />
<br />
I would not wear this at the beach. <br />
I would not wear this while riding a Harley - but maybe while riding a BMW. <br />
<br />
This has the whiff of money, but is also modest and not try hard. <br />
<br />
Some wear it as a signature, I don’t see it as a Swiss Army knife fragrance, it’s not an anytime, handle it all “stick a broom up my ass, I’ll sweep up while I’m at it” type fragrance. This one definitely has it’s times and places. <br />
<br />
It’s a must have  <br />
<br />
Makes a great impression <br />
<br />
The scent itself is just like everyone says, it’s clean and soapy, but it’s more than that. Words aren’t enough.  You have to get your nose on it.  It’s something else, I can’t pretend to know what it is, it all just comes together, like they caught lightning in a bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="1552061"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=1552061#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent727913" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Very strong iris note, more fresh and "clean" then dior homme, not saying one it's better then the other, they're diferente fragrances. It's seems strong and projects well, but I need to test it more because this is probably bottle worth it.<br />
<br />
Infusion iris and iris cedre are also very good but this one is more masculine which I prefer and seems to perform better, and that's always good.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="727913"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=727913#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="39029" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1063104">DrNDJas</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-06-15">06/15/18 21:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Finally tested after all the hype around this one. Not “soapy” at all.  I don’t know where that common description originated for this fragrance, but I’ve never, ever smelled soap that reminds me of Prada l’homme.  There is something sickly sweet in it that smells quite cloying to me up close, actually.  True, it is not offensive, being an iris/floral, but it also is not a smell I would ever associate with a man of any make or model. Of course many cry “wear whatever you want... scents are genderless.”  Fair enough on both accounts, but cultural associations exist nevertheless. Prada l’Homme challenges those associations, so buy accordingly.  This scent would be equally at “homme” on a woman, for sure, even more so than a man. Reading the description from the house, Prada intended for l’Homme to come across this way.  Try as I may, after several attempts, I just don’t enjoy this fragrance at all.  Can’t love em all, sadly.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="952886"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=952886#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent758003" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/153805">mshilov</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-11-03">11/03/16 12:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It looks like Prada made a serious investment in branding (three logos on the bottle and the cap - really too many even for this label) and making a statement with the bottle (ridiculously excessively heavy with enormous 'canvas leather' wrapping), but unfortunately not in fragrance itself. Both scents from this duo are generic and soulless, and even the formal suit by Prada has more soul and charisma than this 'emblematic scent'. It feels all and nothing mixed together in a helpless attempt to please not-very-demanding audience of shopping malls and department stores instead of bringing something new and exciting to the brand's legacy, following it's DNA and discreet Prada perfumery art of the past. This scent bears the name which it doesn't deserve. Launched by mistake - that's how I take it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39029"comment_id="758003"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-39029.html?ccid=758003#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="39029" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
